CREATE PROCEDURE PGFILE/CRTJRN3FILE ( 
	IN PLIBRARY CHAR(10) , 
	IN PFILE CHAR(10) , 
	IN PEXTLIBRARY CHAR(10) , 
	IN PEXTFILE CHAR(10) ) 
	LANGUAGE SQL 
	SPECIFIC PGFILE/CRTJRN3FILE 
	NOT DETERMINISTIC 
	MODIFIES SQL DATA 
	CALLED ON NULL INPUT 
	SET OPTION  ALWBLK = *ALLREAD , 
	ALWCPYDTA = *OPTIMIZE , 
	COMMIT = *NONE , 
	DBGVIEW = *SOURCE , 
	DECRESULT = (31, 31, 00) , 
	DYNDFTCOL = *NO , 
	DYNUSRPRF = *USER , 
	SQLCURRULE = *STD , 
	SRTSEQ = *HEX   
	MAINBODY : BEGIN 
DECLARE VFIRSTCOLUMN VARCHAR ( 128 ) ; 
DECLARE STMT VARCHAR ( 128 ) ; 
DECLARE SQLERRM VARCHAR ( 256 ) DEFAULT '' ; 
DECLARE ERRORINDICATOR CHAR ( 1 ) DEFAULT 'N' ; 
  
SET STMT = '
    SET vfirstColumn = (SELECT column_name 
                          FROM qsys2.syscolumns 
                         WHERE table_schema = "APOC" 
                           AND table_name = "TRNSFRP"
                           AND ordinal_position = 1)' ; 
PREPARE S1 FROM STMT ; 
EXECUTE S1 ; 
END MAINBODY  ;

	MLRCEN , 
	MLRDAT , 
	MLRTIM , 
	MLFILE , 
	MLLIB , 
	MLFTYP , 
	MLFILA , 
	MLMXD , 
	MLFATR , 
	MLSYSN , 
	MLASP , 
	MLRES ,

	MLNAME , 
	MLNRCD , 
	MLNDTR , 
	MLSIZE , 
	MLSEU , 
	MLCCEN , 
	MLCDAT , 
	MLCHGC , 
	MLCHGD , 
	MLCHGT , 
	MLMTXT , 
	MLSEU2 , 
	MLUCEN , 
	MLUDAT , 
	MLUCNT , 
	MLTCEN , 
	MLTDAT , 
	MLSIZ2 , 
	MLSTFR )

	MLRCEN , 
	MLRDAT , 
	MLRTIM , 
	MLFILE , 
	MLLIB , 
	MLFTYP ,

	MLTDAT ,
